beginState: s32'MP'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    deactivateObjectByNameExceptSelf: s32'MP'
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
    upon: (SIGNAL_EX)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(1)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(SignalParam)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(2)
        calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X), (PLAYER), (PLAYER_LAND), (ENEMY), (PLAYER_LAND)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Mem(Tmp)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg4), Val(750000)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(100)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ActReg4), Val(750000)
          modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ActReg4), Val(25000)
          ifNot: Mem(ActReg4)
            storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(1)
          endIf: 
          modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Val(100), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg4)
        endElse: 
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(SignalParam), Mem(ActReg4)
        modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(Tmp), Val(100)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(7)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(SignalParam)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(3)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_72'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(4)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_72'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(5)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_82'
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_02'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(6)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_83'
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_68_1'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (FRAME_STEP)
      ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal1)
        if: Mem(BattleDoing)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg0), (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
          checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Special_MP'
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg1)
              ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamageOrGuard)
                modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg2)
                modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(125)
                modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(ActReg2)
                storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          if: Mem(ExGauge0)
            defence: -64
          endIf: 
          else: 
            defence: 128
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(PlayerVal1)
        ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
          if: Mem(BattleDoing)
            ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
              ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(CheckStop)
                ifNot: Mem(ActReg3)
                  ifNot: Mem(EXBoss)
                    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(200)
                  endIf: 
                  else: 
                    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(400)
                  endElse: 
                endIf: 
                else: 
                  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
                endElse: 
                ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(42000)
                  defence: -64
                  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
                  storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
                  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg0), (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
                  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      moveToObject: (PLAYER)
      setDepth: 0
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(0)
      if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      ifNot: Mem(BattleDoing)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(25)
        ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(ActionTime), Val(16)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(ActionTime), Val(25)
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Magic'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
            endIf: 
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Magic_air'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  beginLabel: s32'loop'
  sprite: s32'null', 7
  ifNot: Mem(ObjReg4)
    if: Mem(ObjReg0)
      createParticle: s32'ask_MP_cost_down_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ObjReg1)
      createParticle: s32'ask_MP_regeneration_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ObjReg2)
      createParticle: s32'ask_draw_auto_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ObjReg3)
      createParticle: s32'ask_magic_recycle_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'loop'
endState:

  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Mem(FuncArg1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
      ifNot: Mem(EXBoss)
      endIf: 
      else: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(5)
      endElse: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'MP'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    deactivateObjectByNameExceptSelf: s32'MP'
    storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
    upon: (SIGNAL_EX)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(1)
        modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(SignalParam)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(0)
          storeValue: Mem(ExGauge0), Val(1)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(2)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(756000)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg6), Val(50)
        calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_X), (PLAYER), (PLAYER_LAND), (ENEMY), (PLAYER_LAND)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Mem(Tmp)
        ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg5)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(100)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg5)
          modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Val(1366000), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg5)
          modifyVar: (DIV), Mem(ActReg5), Mem(ActReg6)
          modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg5)
          modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Val(100), Mem(Tmp), Mem(ActReg4)
          ifNot: Mem(ActReg4)
            storeValue: Mem(ActReg4), Val(1)
          endIf: 
        endElse: 
        modifyVar2: (MUL), Mem(SignalParam), Mem(ActReg4)
        modifyVar2: (DIV), Mem(Tmp), Val(100)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(Tmp)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(7)
        ifNot: Mem(PlayerDamageOrGuard)
          modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(SignalParam)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(3)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_72'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(4)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_72'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(5)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_82'
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_02'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(6)
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(1)
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_83'
          privateSE: s32'SE_BTL_ASK_68_1'
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg3), Val(0)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (FRAME_STEP)
      ifNot: Mem(PlayerVal1)
        if: Mem(BattleDoing)
          storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
          storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg0), (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
          checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Special_MP'
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg1)
              ifTrueInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(PlayerDamageOrGuard)
                modifyVarAfterOperation: (SUB), Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg2)
                modifyVar: (MUL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(125)
                modifyVar: (SUB), Mem(ExGauge0), Mem(ActReg2)
                storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          if: Mem(ExGauge0)
            defence: -64
          endIf: 
          else: 
            defence: 128
            storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(1)
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      if: Mem(PlayerVal1)
        ifNot: Mem(IsRoundTimerStop)
          if: Mem(BattleDoing)
            ifNot: Mem(IsSomebodysCutScene)
              ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(CheckStop)
                ifNot: Mem(ActReg3)
                  getTrainingItemVal: s32'TRP_ASK00', 2, 157
                  ifNot: Mem(TrainingValue)
                    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(105)
                  endIf: 
                endIf: 
                else: 
                  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
                endElse: 
                ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ExGauge0), Val(42000)
                  defence: -64
                  storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal1), Val(0)
                  storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
                  storeValueFromObject: (SELF), Mem(ActReg0), (PLAYER), Mem(HitPoint)
                  storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
                endIf: 
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
      moveToObject: (PLAYER)
      setDepth: 0
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(0)
      if: Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      ifNot: Mem(BattleDoing)
        storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      ifOperationInObject: (IS_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg0), Val(25)
        ifOperationInObject: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(ActionTime), Val(16)
          ifOperationInObject: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), (PLAYER), Mem(ActionTime), Val(25)
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Magic'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
            endIf: 
            checkCurrentStateName: (PLAYER), s32'Magic_air'
            if: Mem(Tmp)
              storeValue: Mem(ObjReg4), Val(1)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  beginLabel: s32'loop'
  sprite: s32'null', 7
  ifNot: Mem(ObjReg4)
    if: Mem(ObjReg0)
      createParticle: s32'ask_MP_cost_down_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ObjReg1)
      createParticle: s32'ask_MP_regeneration_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ObjReg2)
      createParticle: s32'ask_draw_auto_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
    if: Mem(ObjReg3)
      createParticle: s32'ask_magic_recycle_buff_start', (PLAYER)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  endLabel: 
  gotoLabel: s32'loop'
endState: 

beginSubroutine: s32'set_deck'
  if: Mem(FuncArg0)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg5), Val(0)
    ifNot: Mem(ObjReg0)
      ifNot: Mem(ObjReg1)
        ifNot: Mem(ObjReg2)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Val(1111111111)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Val(1111111111)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Val(1111111111)
          storeValue: Mem(ObjReg5), Val(30)
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(FuncArg1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ObjReg0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ObjReg1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ObjReg2)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(FuncArg2)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg0), Mem(ActReg0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg1), Mem(ActReg0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg2), Mem(ActReg0)
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(FuncArg3)
    stackObjectEx: (SELF), (STACK0), 3, (STACK6)
    upon: (PRE_FRAME_STEP)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg6), Val(10000)
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'draw_init'
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(0)
  ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(ActReg5), Val(250)
    setRandom: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1), Val(3)
    setRandom: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1), Val(10)
  endIf: 
  else: 
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(11)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(4)
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
  endElse: 
  modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg5), Val(1)
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'draw_magic'
  if: Mem(ActReg0)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000000000)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(10)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000000000), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD_EQUALS_0), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1000000000)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(9)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(100000000), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-100000000)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(8)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(10000000), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-10000000)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(7)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000000), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1000000)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(6)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(100000), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-100000)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(10000), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-10000)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(4)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1000), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1000)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(100), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-100)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(2)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(10), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-10)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
      modifyVarAfterOperation: (DIV), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Mem(ActReg3)
      ifOperation: (MOD), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1)
        returnValue: 0, 1
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(-1000000000)
  endIf: 
endSubroutine: 

beginSubroutine: s32'set_magic'
  if: Mem(FuncArg0)
    modifyVarAfterOperation: (MUL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(10), Mem(ActReg4)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg4), Mem(ActReg2)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(1)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg4), Val(-10)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(2)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg4), Val(40)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal0), Val(3)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg4), Val(90)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg0), (SELF), Mem(ActReg4)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg1), (SELF), Mem(ActReg4)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(3)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg2), (SELF), Mem(ActReg4)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(4)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg3), (SELF), Mem(ActReg4)
    endIf: 
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'Magic_cost', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    endRunOnObject: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 1
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 2
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(10)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(3)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 3
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(100)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(4)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 4
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg6), Val(1000)
    endIf: 
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg5), Val(-1)
  endIf: 
  if: Mem(FuncArg1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg0), (SELF), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg1), (SELF), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(3)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg2), (SELF), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(4)
      storeValueFromObject: (PLAYER), Mem(ObjReg3), (SELF), Val(0)
    endIf: 
    runOnObject: (PLAYER)
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'Magic_cost', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    endRunOnObject: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(1)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 1
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(2)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 2
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(3)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 3
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalParam), Val(4)
      sendSignalEx: (STACK0), 0, 4
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

  ignoreSuperFreezeFromAlly: 1

      setPositionYByScreenPercentage: 90

        endElse: 
      endIf:

  endUpon: 
endSubroutine:

  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    deactivateObjectByNameExceptSelf: s32'deck1'
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'set_deck', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(1)
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'null', 2147483647
  upon: (SIGNAL_EX)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SignalID), Val(0)
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'set_deck', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
      beginLabel: s32'loop'
      callSubroutine: s32'draw_init'

      callSubroutine: s32'draw_magic'

      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'set_deck', Val(0), Val(0), Val(1), Val(0)
      callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'set_magic', Val(1), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    endIf:

      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject1), Val(1)

          setPositionXByScreenPercentage: 28
        endIf:

          setPositionXByScreenPercentage: 31

        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(1)
          setPositionXByScreenPercentage: 29
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(2)
          setPositionXByScreenPercentage: 32
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(3)
          setPositionXByScreenPercentage: 35
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(SentToObject0), Val(4)
          setPositionXByScreenPercentage: 38
        endIf: 
        storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Mem(ActReg2)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(0)
        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number0'
      endIf:

        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number1'
      endIf:

        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number2'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(3)
        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number3'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(4)
        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number4'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(5)
        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number5'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(6)
        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number6'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(7)
        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number7'
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(8)
        linkParticle: s32'cmn_number8'

beginSubroutine: s32'CubeMagicLimit'
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(1)
    storeValue: Mem(ActReg3), Mem(FuncArg1)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(5)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(10)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(1)
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(3)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Mem(SentToObject0)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg2), Val(3)
    endIf: 
    upon: (SIGNAL0)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Mem(ActReg1)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL0)
        clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL1)
        deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
      findState: s32'AttackMagic_03_Main', 4, 2, 47
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
      findState: s32'AttackMagic_05_Main', 4, 2, 47
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(3)
      findState: s32'AttackMagic_10_Main', 4, 2, 47
    endIf: 
    isObjectActive: (STACK0)
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      sendSignal: (STACK0), (SIGNAL1)
    endIf: 
    upon: (SIGNAL1)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL1)
      clearRegisteredUponCode: (SIGNAL0)
      deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
    endUpon: 
    upon: (PLAYER_RECEIVE_ATTACK)
      sendSignal: (SELF), (SIGNAL1)
    endUpon: 
    upon: (WALL_BREAK)
      sendSignal: (SELF), (SIGNAL1)
    endUpon: 
    upon: (ON_DELETE)
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(1)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(2)
        sendSignal: (STACK0), (SIGNAL0)
      endIf: 
      ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg3), Val(3)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(2)
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg1), Val(1)
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_RAW), (SELF), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (CENTER)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(2500000)
          requestDestroy: (SELF)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
    ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg1), Val(2)
      upon: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        calcDistanceEx: (DISTANCE_RAW), (SELF), (PLAYER), (PLAYER), (CENTER)
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(Tmp), Val(2500000)
          requestDestroy: (SELF)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
        endIf: 
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActionTime), Val(2)
          isObjectActive: (PARENT)
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            requestDestroy: (SELF)
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (NO_STOP_IDLING)
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
      endUpon: 
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(FuncArg0), Val(3)
    modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(1)
    upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
      storeValue: Mem(PlayerVal5), Mem(ObjReg7)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(-1)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(0)
        sendSignalEx: (PLAYER), 1, 0
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(PlayerVal4), Val(10)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_01', (SIGNAL0)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_02', (SIGNAL0)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_03', (SIGNAL0)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_05', (SIGNAL0)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_06', (SIGNAL0)
      sendSignalToAction: s32'AttackMagic_10', (SIGNAL0)
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Mem(PlayerVal4)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(-1)
    endIf: 
    else: 
      storeValue: Mem(ObjReg7), Mem(PlayerVal4)
    endElse: 
    upon: (SIGNAL0)
      modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(-1)
      ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(0)
        requestDestroy: (SELF)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    upon: (SIGNAL1)
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ObjReg7), Mem(PlayerVal5)
        modifyVar: (ADD), Mem(ObjReg7), Val(-1)
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
  endIf: 
endSubroutine:

beginState: s32'ASK_FinishCamera_Pattern'
  ifNotInObject: (PLAYER), Mem(CmnCharaReg3)
    if: Mem(CmnCharaReg5)
      createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Screen_Effect', (PLAYER)
      cameraShakeEX: s32'Depth', 500, 0, 150, 0, s32'shake_easeout'
    endIf: 
    else: 
      ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(600000)
        stackObjectEx: (SELF), (STACK0), 14, (ATTACKER)
        isObjectActive: (STACK0)
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          ifTrueInObject: (STACK0), Mem(IsPlayer)
            setRandom: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Val(3)
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
              createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near01', (PLAYER)
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
              createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Far03', (PLAYER)
            endIf: 
            ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(3)
              createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Far04', (PLAYER)
            endIf: 
          endIf: 
          else: 
            createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Projectile', (PLAYER)
          endElse: 
        endIf: 
        else: 
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Projectile', (PLAYER)
        endElse: 
      endIf: 
      else: 
        ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDiffY), Val(120000)
          createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Up', (PLAYER)
        endIf: 
        else: 
          ifOperation: (IS_LESSER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(EnemyDiffY), Val(-40000)
            createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Down', (PLAYER)
          endIf: 
          else: 
            ifOperation: (IS_LESSER), Mem(EnemyDistanceX), Val(300000)
              setRandom: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Val(2)
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Zoom', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near02', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
            endIf: 
            else: 
              setRandom: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1), Val(2)
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near01', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
              ifOperation: (IS_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg0), Val(2)
                createObject: s32'cmn_FinishCamera_Near02', (PLAYER)
              endIf: 
            endElse: 
          endElse: 
        endElse: 
      endElse: 
    endElse: 
  endIf: 
  createObject: s32'cmnCam_FinishTimeOut', (PLAYER)
  deactivateObjectById: (SELF)
endState:

endState:
